[30;1m30 | [0m[35m=====[0m
[30;1m31 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m32 | [0m[35m``skops`` is a Python library helping you share your `scikit-learn[0m
[30;1m33 | [0m[35m<https://scikit-learn.org/stable/>`__ based models and put them in production.[0m
[30;1m34 | [0m[35mAt the moment, it includes tools to easily integrate models on the Hugging Face[0m
[30;1m35 | [0m[35mHub, which allows you to share your models, make them discoverable, and use the[0m
[30;1m36 | [0m[35mHub's API inference and widgets to get outputs of the model without having to[0m
[30;1m37 | [0m[35mdownload or load the model.[0m

[30;1m88 | [0m[35m=====[0m
[30;1m89 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m90 | [0m[35m``skops`` is a Python library helping you share your `scikit-learn[0m
[30;1m91 | [0m[35m<https://scikit-learn.org/stable/>`__ based models and put them in production.[0m
[30;1m92 | [0m[35mAt the moment, it includes tools to easily integrate models on the Hugging Face[0m
[30;1m93 | [0m[35mHub, which allows you to share your models, make them discoverable, and use the[0m
[30;1m94 | [0m[35mHub's API inference and widgets to get outputs of the model without having to[0m
[30;1m95 | [0m[35mdownload or load the model.[0m

[30;1m10 | [0m[35m<https://scikit-learn.org/stable/>`__ based models and put them in production.[0m
[30;1m11 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m13 | [0m[35mfind the source code and the development discussions on `Github[0m
